***жатва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жатва.html>жа́тва</a> (23554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жѧтва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žętva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žętva</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žęti</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tva</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жатва.html>жа́тва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žátva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жатва.html>жа́твы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жатва.html>жа́твы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жатва.html>жа́тв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>harvest <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">process of harvesting, gathering the ripened crop, harvest yield</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жатый.html>жа́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p>

***жать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a> (7091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žęti</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жѧти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žęti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, 1sg. <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жьмѫ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žĭmǫ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжать.html>сжать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожать.html>пожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press, to squeeze
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žatʹ</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shake hands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to benchpress, to lift</li>
<li>to pinch, to hurt, to be tight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обувь.html>о́бувь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жмёт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">óbuvʹ <b>žmjót</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the shoes are tight (<i>too small</i>)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to press out, to squeeze out</li>
<li>to oppress, to draw near
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>сро́ки</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жму́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sróki <b>žmut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">we are reaching the deadline</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žęti</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жѧти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žęti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, 1sg. <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жьнѭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žĭnjǫ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжать.html>сжать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожать.html>пожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reap, to crop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посеять.html>посе́ешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пожать.html>пожнёшь</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što poséješʹ, to i <b>požnjóšʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">as you sow, so shall you reap</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жаться.html>жа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to huddle up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаться.html>жа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>холода</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žátʹsja</b> ot xoloda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to huddle up with cold</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to draw close <i>(to)</i>, to huddle up <i>(to)</i>, to cuddle up <i>(to)</i>, to nestle up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crowd together</li>
<li>to shrink <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаться.html>жа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерешительность.html>нереши́тельности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žátʹsja</b> v nerešítelʹnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dillydally; balk</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаться.html>жа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>двери</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žátʹsja</b> u dveri</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hang around the door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаться.html>жа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žátʹsja</b> v úgol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shrink into a corner</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be stingy, to stint, to pinch and save
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жаться.html>жми́сь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>бери́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>žmisʹ</b>, berí što xóčešʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't stint yourself; take all you want</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сжаться.html>сжа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sžátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пожа́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">požátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***жбан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жбан.html>жбан</a> (20963)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьbanъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жбан.html>жбан</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žban</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жбан.html>жба́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жбан.html>жба́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жбан.html>жба́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(a large) can; pitcher</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">third-person plural present indicative imperfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жгу́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.

***ждать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a> (202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьdati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wait, to await</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*g(e)id-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰidʰ-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">gīt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">avarice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">gēide</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">they are waiting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ždatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подождать.html>подожда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wait, to wait for (<i>+ genitive case</i>)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1955</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_Nabokov" class="extiw" title="w:Vladimir Nabokov">Vladimir Nabokov</a>,  chapter 14, in  <cite>Lolita</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решённый.html>решено́</a> Лолиту <a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ближайший.html>ближа́йший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четверг.html>четве́рг</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:вместо.html>вме́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:намеченный.html>наме́чен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сначала.html>снача́ла</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Rešenó Lolitu otprávitʹ tudá že v bližájšij četvérg. Vmésto tovó, štóby <b>ždatʹ</b> do ijúlja, kak býlo naméčen snačála.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Lolita, it was decided, would be sent there on Thursday instead of <b>waiting</b> until July, as was initially planned.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>Ждать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>войны́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ždatʹ</b> koncá vojný.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">To wait for the end of the war.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to expect, to await</li></ol>

***же.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> (27)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*že</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*ge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰi</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">že</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γε</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ge</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">हि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">že</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">contrasting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> and, but</li>
<li>whereas, as for, as to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">он—америка́нец, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сская</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On—amerikánec, oná <b>že</b> rússkaja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s an American, <b>whereas</b> she's Russian.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">že</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Emphasises identity</span>: very, same
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">takój <b>že</b> (sámyj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the same, similar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>таку́ю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja kupíl takúju <b>že</b> knígu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I bought <b>the same</b> book.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tot <b>že</b> (sámyj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the same, identical</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On vsjó tot <b>že</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's always <b>the same</b>!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мое</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto tó <b>že</b> sámoje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It's <b>the same</b> thing.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">With expressions of time and order: emphasises promptitude</span>: very, right, immediately, without delay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страница.html>страни́це</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бка</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na pérvoj <b>že</b> straníce bylá ošíbka.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Right</b> on the first page there was a mistake.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дующий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́ва</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na slédujuščij <b>že</b> denʹ rabóta bylá gotóva.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The <b>very</b> next day the work was finished.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прекратить.html>прекрати́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Prekratíte sejčás <b>že</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stop <b>immediately</b>!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>После</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужин.html>у́жина</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>легла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Posle úžina oná srázu <b>že</b> leglá spatʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After dinner she went <b>straight</b> to bed.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Makes an objection by pointing to an obvious fact</span>: after all, but
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ете</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>Э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Počemú vy ne ponimájete? Eto <b>že</b> rússkij!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why don't you understand? <b>After all</b>, it’s Russian!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">-Я <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a>. -Я <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">-Ja ne znal, što závtra ekzámen. -Ja <b>že</b> tebé skazál!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">-I didn't know the exam was tomorrow. -<b>But</b> I told you!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Especially in questions: expresses consequence of or reaction to what was said before</span>: then, so
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što ž?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>then</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što ž!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Well <b>then</b>!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kogdá <b>že</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">When <b>then</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>Где</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Gde <b>že</b> éto?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Where is it <b>then</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu što <b>že</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What of it, <b>then</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu i što <b>ž</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Well</b>, what of it? / <b>So</b> what?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što <b>ž</b> iz étovo?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What of it?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лает</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što <b>ž</b>, on sam éto sdélajet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Why</b>, he'll just do it himself!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">In questions and imperatives: imparts a note of insistence and urgency</span>: ever, on earth, for goodness' sake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što <b>že</b> jemú délatʹ?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>on earth</b> can he do?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́те</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Govoríte <b>že</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Aren’t you going to say anything!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвечать.html>отвеча́йте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otvečájte <b>že</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Answer me <b>then</b>!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>Пойдём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pojdjóm <b>že</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Come along!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">že</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>zhe: <span class="use-with-mention">The name of the Cyrillic-script letter</span> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>Ж</a></b>.</li>
<li>gee: <span class="use-with-mention">The name of the Latin-script letter</span> <b>G</b>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">гэ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gɛ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b></b>

Зализняка).

***жевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жевать.html>жева́ть</a> (3272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьvati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to chew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǴiewH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жевать.html>жева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ževátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожевать.html>пожева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to chew, to munch</li>
<li>to ruminate, to masticate</li>
<li>to repeat with tiresome monotony, to repeat something monotonously</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">želánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">želánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>desired, desirable, welcome, sought-after</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лан.html>ла́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>жела́ннее, жела́нней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-жела-</b>; суффикс: <b>-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">želátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ла́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a> (972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*želàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">želátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожелать.html>пожела́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возжелать.html>возжела́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wish, to desire</li>
<li>to covet</li>
<li>to wish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добра́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>želátʹ</b> dobrá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wish well</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>želátʹ</b> udáči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wish good luck</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>želátʹ</b> zla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bear ill will</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">желѣзо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">želězo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*želězo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>желе́зо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">želézo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>желе́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>желе́за</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>желе́з</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>iron</li>
<li>any iron-like metal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computer slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hardware</li></ol>

***желтеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:желтеть.html>желте́ть</a> (11230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желтый.html>жёлтый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žóltyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰelh₃-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yellow; gleam; to shine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gild</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">glow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желтеть.html>желте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">želtétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожелтеть.html>пожелте́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become yellow</li>
<li>to show yellow, to be seen, to be visible</li></ol>
